<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科明厭離，說明那時眾生起上厭離。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">爾時有情展轉聚集，起上厭離，不復退減。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那時有情受不了，實在是太苦了，就展轉聚集在一起商議對策，於是生起上品的厭離心，壽量就不再退減。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《法華經玄贊要集》卷19說：「好殺眾生，多生刀兵劫中，人心最惡，草木化成刀劍。」喜好殺生的人，將來多生刀兵劫中，因為這種人心最不好，草木碰到他都變成可以殺人的刀劍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《佛說樓閣正法甘露鼓經》卷1說：「若有人一日持此遠離殺生之戒，彼人不生刀兵劫中。」如果有情能受持不殺生戒，將來就不會生到刀兵劫中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天四、明受行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科明受行，說明受行善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又能棄捨損減壽量惡不善法，受行增長壽量善法。由此因緣，壽量、色力、富樂、自在皆漸增長，乃至壽量經八萬歲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦到極點，終於知道要修行了。那些有情就棄捨使壽量減損的殺生、偷盜、邪淫、妄語等這些惡不善法，接著受行增長壽量的十善法。由此因緣，那些有情壽命的數量、色相身力、富貴安樂與生活的自在力，慢慢地又增長，乃至回到八萬歲時的勝妙境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、例滿住劫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例滿住劫，以一個減劫、一個增劫，各滿二十個就是住劫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是二十減、二十增，合四十增減，便出住劫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上減劫及增劫的相狀，經過二十個減劫，二十個增劫，合起來四十個增減，就出住劫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、壞劫攝2　申一、有情世間壞2　酉一、惡趣壞2　戌一、舉那落迦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一科壞劫攝，說明壞劫所攝，分二科；第一科有情世間壞，說明有情的世間壞，又分二科；第一科惡趣壞，說明惡趣壞，又分二科；第一科舉那落迦，舉地獄先壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於最後增已，爾時那落迦有情唯沒不生。如是漸漸乃至沒盡，當知說名那落迦世間壞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於最後增劫時，地獄的有情死了以後就不再出生。如是漸漸所有地獄的有情全部死掉了，這個地獄的世間就壞掉了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、例傍生等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例傍生等，例說旁生等壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p135"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如那落迦壞，傍生、餓鬼壞亦如是。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　到住劫最後，地獄壞了，畜生、餓鬼道也一樣會壞掉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、善趣壞2　戌一、舉人趣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科善趣壞，說明善趣壞所攝，分二科；第一科舉人趣，舉人趣為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="50705:1195"></a>爾時人中隨一有情，自然法爾所得第二靜慮。其餘有情展轉隨學，亦復如是。皆此沒已，生極淨光天眾同分中。當知爾時說名人世間壞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那時人中隨其中一位有情，自然就會成就第二禪。其他的有情展轉跟這位有情學習，也都能夠修得二禪的境界。人間的有情死了，都生到二禪的極淨光天眾同分中。應當知道那時稱為人世間壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、例天趣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例天趣，如人趣壞，天趣的有情也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如人趣既爾，天趣亦然。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如人趣有情，天趣的有情也一樣，死了就生到二禪天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、器世間壞2　酉一、正壞2　戌一、明漸次</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科器世間壞，壞劫開始時，器世間壞，分二科；第一科正壞，正在壞時，又分二科；第一科明漸次，說明壞的漸次。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當於此時，五趣世間居住之處無一有情可得，所有資具亦不可得。非唯資具不可復得，爾時天雨亦不可得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　當世間要壞時，就是一般說的世界末日，那時五趣世間居住之處，沒有一個有情可得，沒有地獄、沒有畜生、沒有餓鬼、沒有人，也沒有天，所有生活的資具都不可得。不只所有生活的資具不可得，這時天也不下雨，乾旱了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋所由2　亥一、別辨相2　天一、由無雨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所由，解釋原因，分二科；第一科別辨相，各別說明乾旱的相狀，又分二科；第一科由無雨，因為沒有雨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由無雨故，大地所有藥草叢林皆悉枯槁。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為沒有下雨，大地所有的藥草、樹木、叢林通通都枯萎了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、由熱增2　地一、此日輪</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由熱增，因為熱度增加，分二科；第一科此日輪，太陽熱度增加。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復由無雨之所攝故，令此日輪熱勢增大。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又因為那時沒有下雨，所以使令太陽的熱力增大。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p136"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、餘日輪3　玄一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科餘日輪，其他的太陽出現，分三科；第一科標，標出還有六個太陽出現。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸有情能感壞劫業增上力故，及依六種所燒事故，復有六日輪漸次而現。彼諸日輪望舊日輪所有熱勢，踰前四倍。既成七已，熱遂增七。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由有情造作能感壞劫共業的增上力，還有六種所燒事的緣故，包括河水、溝渠、大海等，被燒的事情有六種，又有六個太陽漸次會出現。每一個太陽在出現時，相對於原來的那個太陽，所有的熱度超過前面太陽的四倍。既然有七個太陽，每個比現在的太陽熱度增加四倍，四的六次方，加起來是4096倍的熱度。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為六所燒事？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為六所燒事？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄三、釋2　黃一、諸水枯竭</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科諸水枯竭，說明諸水枯竭的現象。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、小大溝坑，由第二日輪之所枯竭；二、小河大河，由第三日輪之所枯竭；三、無熱大池，由第四日輪之所枯竭；四者、大海，由第五日輪及第六一分之所枯竭；</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、小大溝坑，由第二個太陽的高熱照射，全部晒乾枯竭；二、小河大河，世間上大小河流，由第三個太陽的高熱照射，全部晒乾枯竭；三、無熱大池，什麼是無熱大池？《長阿含經》卷18說：通常龍都有三種熱惱，第一種是熱風與熱沙，燒龍的皮肉骨髓，令牠痛苦而生熱惱；第二是惡風暴起，龍的資具、宮殿都被吹壞，龍身就會現前生起熱惱；第三個是金翅鳥，牠會將龍子與龍女全部吃掉，令龍生熱惱。這條龍沒有這種熱惱，稱為無熱，也稱為阿耨達。無熱住的大池稱為無熱大池，是由第四個太陽的高熱照射而全部晒乾枯竭；四、大海，如太平洋、大西洋、印度洋等，由第五個太陽及第六個太陽的一部分出現時，高熱照射而全部晒乾枯竭。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、大地燒然2　宇一、出所燒</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科大地燒燃，大地被燒掉，分二科；第一科出所燒，說出為第六一分及第七日輪之所燒燃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">六、蘇迷盧山及以大地，體堅實故，由第六一分及第七日輪之所燒然。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六 、蘇迷盧山（又稱作須彌山或妙高山）及大地的體性堅實，由第六個太陽的一部分及第七個太陽出來時，在最高的熱度下全部燒光，這時世間就燒壞了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、明邊際</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明邊際，說明燒壞的邊際。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此火焰為風所鼓，展轉熾盛，極至梵世。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這個火焰被風所鼓動，展轉的越來越大，最高燒到初禪天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p137"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、略攝事2　天一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科略攝事，要略歸為三事，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出三事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又如是等，略為三事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這些被燒壞的東西，可以要略歸納為三件事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、列釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列出來解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、水所生事，謂藥草等，由初所槁；二、即水事，由五所涸；三、恆相續住體堅實事，由二所燒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、水所生事，指藥草等，由第一個太陽晒乾枯竭；二、水事，包括小大溝坑、小河大河，無熱大池及大海，由中間五個太陽所燒掉；三、恆相續住體堅實事，世間最高大的蘇迷盧山及大地，由第六個太陽的一部分及第七個太陽出來燒掉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、已壞2　戌一、證壞劫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科已壞，說明世間已壞，分二科；第一科證壞劫，證明壞劫現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是世界皆悉燒已，乃至灰燼及與餘影皆不可得，廣說如經。從此名為器世間已壞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說，壞劫時，七個太陽都出來了，又沒有下雨，這世間全部被燒壞了，燒到連灰燼及影子也不可得，地水火風都看不到，詳細情形如經所說。從此名為器世間已壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》乃至灰燼及與餘影皆不可得廣說如經者：增一阿含經中七日品說：若復七日出時，此須彌山漸漸融壞，百千由旬自然崩落，永無有餘，亦復不見塵烟之分，況見灰乎。此說灰燼及與餘影，隨應可知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《增一阿含經》中〈七日品〉說：若第七個太陽出來時，須彌山就漸漸地被太陽的熱度融化破壞，百千由旬高的山就自然崩塌掉落，不會留下一點點的土在上面，也看不到一點點微細的塵煙之類，連煙都看不到，何況看到灰呢。此處說灰燼及與餘影都不可得，參考《增一阿含經》的〈七日品〉就可以知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">滿足二十中劫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是壞劫，時間也有二十中劫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、顯空劫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯空劫，說明空劫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p138"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是壞已，復二十中劫住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　壞劫以後，空劫也是二十個中劫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、水災2　午一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科水災，說明水災，分二科；第一科徵，先問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何水災？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是水災？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋2　未一、壞劫攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科壞劫攝，為壞劫所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂過七火災已，於第二靜慮中，有俱生水界起，壞器世間，如水消鹽。此之水界與器世間一時俱沒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經過七個火災以後（七次的成住壞空，就是七大劫），在第二禪天當中，有俱生的水界生起，將二禪天的器世間破壞，宮殿被水消融，好像水將鹽溶掉一樣。大水起來時，就將二禪天以下的器世間一起淹沒了。這時是第八個大劫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、空劫攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科空劫攝，說明還有二十中劫空劫住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是沒已，復二十中劫住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　水災壞器世間後，接著還有二十中劫的空劫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、風災2　午一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科風災，說明風災的相狀，分二科；第一科徵，問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何風災？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是風災？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋2　未一、壞劫攝2　申一、標彼相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科壞劫攝，說明壞劫所攝，又分二科；第一科標彼相，標出風災的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂七水災過已，復七火災；從此無間，於第三靜慮中有俱生風界起，壞器世間，如風乾支節，復能消盡。此之風界與器世間一時俱沒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七個水災（一個水災有八大劫）過了，還有七個火災，七乘八等於五十六，再加上七個火災，就等於六十三，再加上一個風災，第六十四大劫時，風災起來就將第三靜慮天中的器世間全都吹壞，就像風會使有情的支節被風乾燥，最後被侵蝕盡滅。風界破壞器世間，與器世間一時俱沒，也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p139"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、顯所以</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯所以，開顯風災的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？現見有一由風界發，乃令其骨皆悉消盡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼會這樣？因為現前可見有人風濕病發作時，不但全身疼痛，連骨頭都被風蝕殆盡。如果去過海邊可以看到，岸邊的岩石被海風侵蝕，日益減損，最後全被風蝕掉了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、空劫攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科空劫攝，說明空劫所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從此壞已，復二十中劫住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六十四大劫的壞劫後，還會有二十中劫的空劫住。成住壞空的道理都是一樣的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、世間成2　辰一、結前生後</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科世間成，說明世間成劫時的相狀，分二科；第一科結前生後，結束前文，生起後文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="20812:1243"></a>如是略說世間已壞。云何世間成？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文已經略說，器世間將壞時有火、水、風大三災。火災每一大劫就發生一次，水災是每八大劫發生一次，風劫是六十四大劫發生一次。壞劫後，還會有二十中劫的空劫住，接著進入成劫，稱為世間成。開始有世間時，是如何成就的呢？以前念的書是說世間一開始沒有人居住，後來有猿猴，再進化變成人類，現在經文不是那樣敘述。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、廣辨一切2　巳一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣辨一切，詳細說明成劫的一切相狀，分二科；第一科總標，總標由眾生共業所感。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂過如是二十中劫已，一切有情業增上力故，世間復成。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過了二十中劫的空劫以後，由一切有情的共業所感，世間又開始形成。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、別顯2　午一、下三靜慮攝2　未一、器世間2　申一、舉第三靜慮</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別顯，各別的顯示，分二科；第一科下三靜慮攝，說明下三靜慮攝，又分二科；第一科器世間，說明器世間，又分二科；第一科舉第三靜慮，先舉第三靜慮器世間的形成。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">爾時最初於虛空中，第三靜慮器世間成。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那時最初在虛空中，第三靜慮開始有器世間出現。在風劫時，最後被破壞的是第三禪天，器世間成也是從第三禪天開始，因為最後壞、最先成。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、例餘靜慮</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘靜慮，推例其餘靜慮器世間的形成。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如第三靜慮，第二及初亦復如是。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與第三禪天一樣，漸漸地，第二禪天的器世間也成了，然後初禪天的器世間也成了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、有情世間3　申一、第三靜慮2　酉一、舉上品生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有情世間，說明有情世間的形成，分三科；第一科第三靜慮，說明第三禪天的有情，又分二科；第一科舉上品生，說明上品生的有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p140"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">爾時第三災頂有諸有情由壽盡故，業盡故，福盡故，從彼沒已，生第三靜慮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那時第三災風災頂，第四禪天的人，他們的壽量盡了，業盡了，或是福報盡了，從四禪天死了，就生到第三禪天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、例餘品生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘品生，推例餘品類生的有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">餘一切處，漸次亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　福報更低的人，又生到第二禪天，或是初禪天等，次第也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、第二靜慮2　酉一、舉上品生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二靜慮，說明第二靜慮，分二科；第一科舉上品生，舉上品生有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復從第二災頂生第二靜慮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三禪天的人壽盡、業盡、福盡，就生到二禪天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、例餘品生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘品生，推例餘品類生的有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">餘一切處，應知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二禪天的人壽盡、業盡、福盡，就生到初禪天等去。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、初靜慮2　酉一、大梵生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科初靜慮，說明初靜慮的有情，分二科；第一科大梵生，說明大梵天王先生出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復從第一災頂，有一有情由壽等盡故，從彼沒已，生初靜慮梵世界中，為最大梵。由獨一故，而懷不悅。便有希望：今當云何令餘有情亦來生此。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從第一災頂的二禪天，有一個有情因壽盡、業盡、福盡，在第二禪天死了，就生到初禪天，為大梵天王。因為只有一個人，他心裡不高興。一個人活著也很苦悶，便有希望：應當令其他的有情也來初禪天和我作伴。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、餘梵生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科餘梵生，說明其餘梵天生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當發心時，諸餘有情由壽等盡故，從第二靜慮沒已，生初靜慮彼同分中。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　當大梵天王這樣發心時，其他在第二禪天的有情，因壽盡、業盡、福盡死了，就生到初靜慮與他作伴。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、欲界諸趣攝2　未一、空居四天2　申一、器世間</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科欲界諸趣攝，說明欲界諸趣所攝，分二科；第一科空居四天，說明空居四天，又分二科；第一科器世間，先說器世間。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p141"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是下三靜慮器及有情世間成已，於虛空中，欲界四天宮殿漸成。當知彼諸虛空宮殿皆如化出。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是下三靜慮器世間及有情世間成就以後，虛空中有欲界的四天宮殿（空居天，分為夜摩天、兜率天、化樂天、與他化自在天）漸漸成就。這些虛空宮殿都是變化生出的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、有情世間</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有情世間，說明空居天的有情世間。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸有情，從極淨光天眾同分沒，而來生此諸宮殿中。餘如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這些有情，都是從極淨光天（二禪天）的眾同分中死掉，而來生到這些宮殿中。隨他們的品類上中下，由上至下生至他化自在天、化樂天、兜率天、及夜摩天的宮殿當中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、地居諸趣2　申一、一切器世間2　酉一、約居處辨2　戌一、成漸次3　亥一、風輪2　天一、標依持</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科地居諸趣，說明地居諸趣，分二科；第一科一切器世間，說明一切器世間，又分二科；第一科約居處辨，說明有情的居處，又分二科；第一科成漸次，說明成立器世間的漸次，又分三科；第一科風輪，風輪先起，又分二科；第一科標依持，標出先有大風輪為彼世界作依持。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自此以後，有大風輪，量等三千大千世界，從下而起，與彼世界作所依持，為欲安立無有宮殿諸有情類。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從這以後，有大風輪，其面積等同三千大千世界，從下面生起，這個風輪可以作世界的依持，是為安立沒有宮殿的有情在此安住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋彼相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋彼相，解釋風輪的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此大風輪有二種相。謂仰周布及傍側布，由此持水令不散墜。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這大風輪有二種相貌。一、仰周布，向上吹的，二、傍側布，向旁邊吹的。由下往上吹，由中間往旁邊吹，如此會使水不會散掉下來。如果由上往下，這水就會掉下來，變成下雨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、水輪</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科水輪，先有風輪出現，再來有水輪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次由彼業增上力故，於虛空界金藏雲興。從此降雨，注風輪上。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，由於眾生共業的增上緣力，於虛空中有金藏雲出現。從此下雨，流注在風輪上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、地輪</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科地輪，說明地輪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p142"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復起風，鼓水令堅，此即名為金性地輪。上堪水雨之所激注，下為風飈之所衝薄。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　接下來是風再生起，將水吹著黏在一起，使它成為堅硬的地大，這個稱為金性地輪。地輪上面可以承受雨水的貫注，下面還有很大的風在衝擊著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、成差別2　亥一、出諸處2　天一、蘇迷盧及七金山2　地一、辨體性2　玄一、蘇迷盧2　黃一、舉因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科成差別，說明器世間成的差別相，分二科；第一科出諸處，說明諸處出現，又分二科；第一科蘇迷盧及七金山，先說蘇迷盧山及七金山，又分二科；第一科辨體性，說明蘇迷盧山及七金山的體性，又分二科；第一科蘇迷盧，說明蘇迷盧山，又分二科；第一科舉因，說明成因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此地成已，即由彼業增上力故，空中復起諸界藏雲，又從彼雲降種種雨。然其雨水，乃依金性地輪而住。次復風起，鼓水令堅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　金性的地輪成就後，由眾生共業的增上緣力，在空中會生起地水火風諸界的藏雲，又從藏雲降下種種的雨。雨水就依止此金性的地輪而安住。接下來，風一吹，又令水變成堅硬性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、顯性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯性，說明蘇迷盧山的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即由此風力所引故，諸有清淨第一最勝精妙性者，成蘇迷盧山。此山成已，四寶為體。所謂金、銀、頗胝、琉璃。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於風力所吸引，將水吹成地輪，世間上就有清淨第一最殊勝精妙性者，成為蘇迷盧山。世間最初成就的器世間是蘇迷盧山，最後破壞也是蘇迷盧山。此山成就後，有四寶為其體性，就是金（北邊是黃色）、銀（東邊是白色）、頗胝（西邊是赤色）、琉璃（南邊是青色）。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、七金山3　黃一、標性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科七金山，說明七金山，分三科；第一科標性，標出中品性者成七金山。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若中品性者，成七金山。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說這世間有風輪、水輪，再來地輪長成後，天空下雨就將水吹成蘇迷盧山，這是上品的地輪。中品性清淨的地輪，就成七金山。因為它不是由金、銀、頗胝、琉璃最淨妙的寶物為體。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、列名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列名，列出七金山的名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂持雙山、毗那矺迦山、馬耳山、善見山、朅達洛迦山、持軸山、尼民達羅山。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七金山的名字是：持雙山（山頂上有二個峰）、毗那矺迦山（意指障礙）、馬耳山（像馬耳）、善見山、朅達洛迦山（印度話：擔木）、持軸山（山峰像軸一樣）、尼民達羅山（水中魚的名字）。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p143"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃三、釋相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋相，解釋七金山的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是諸山，其峰布列，各由形狀差別為名，繞蘇迷盧次第而住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些山的分布排列，各依其形狀差別而命名，圍繞在蘇迷盧山次第而立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、顯彼量2　玄一、蘇迷盧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯彼量，說明蘇迷盧山及七金山的量，分二科；第一科蘇迷盧，說明蘇迷盧山的量。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">蘇迷盧量，高八萬踰繕那，廣亦如之，下入水際，量亦復爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘇迷盧山它的量（高度），高度是八萬踰繕那（由旬），廣度也是八萬踰繕那，它也深入到海底，從水平面至海底也是有八萬踰繕那。踰繕那又名由旬，若將由旬配合中國的里數，有很多種說法，其中據《大唐西域記》卷2載，踰繕那乃指聖王一日行軍的路程。舊傳一踰繕那為四十里，印度國俗為三十里，佛教則說十六里。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、七金山2　黃一、持雙山</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科七金山，說明七金山的量，分二科；第一科持雙山，說明持雙山的量。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又持雙山，等彼之半。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　持雙山的量，是蘇迷盧山的一半，是四萬踰繕那（由旬），高廣都一樣，水下也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、餘六山</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科餘六山，說明其他的六金山。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從此次第，餘六金山其量漸減，各等其半。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從此次第，其他六金山其體積漸漸的減半，愈來愈小，各等於前者的一半。第二個毗那矺迦山，據說有天神住在裡頭，障礙善法，二萬由旬；依次減半，馬耳山是一萬由旬、善見山是五千由旬、朅達洛迦山是二千五百由旬、持軸山是一千二百五十由旬、尼民達羅山是六百二十五由旬。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、四大洲等5　地一、四大洲八中洲并輪圍山2　玄一、略標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科四大洲等，說明四大洲等，分五科；第一科四大洲八中洲并輪圍山，說明四大洲、八中洲及輪圍山，又分二科；第一科略標列，要略的標列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若下品性者，於蘇迷盧四邊七金山外，成四大洲及八中洲，并輪圍山。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　更下品的地輪，在蘇迷盧四邊七金山以外，又形成四大洲：東毗提訶洲、南贍部洲、西瞿陀尼洲、北拘盧洲，又有八個中洲，及輪圍山。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、隨別釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨別釋，接著各別的解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此山輪圍四洲而住，量等尼民達羅之半。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此輪圍山圍著四大洲而住，數量只有尼民達羅山的一半，是三百一十二點五由旬。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p144"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、非天宮殿</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科非天宮殿，說明非天宮殿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="3067:1300"></a>復成非天宮殿，此宮在蘇迷盧下，依水而居。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又形成阿修羅的宮殿，在蘇迷盧山的下面，依著入水處而住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、大雪山無熱池</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科大雪山無熱池，說明大雪山的無熱池。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復成大雪山及無熱池周圍崖岸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又形成大雪山及無熱池的周圍崖岸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地四、一切那落迦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科一切那落迦，說明地獄器世間的形成。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次成最下八大那落迦處，諸大那落迦，及獨一那落迦、寒那落迦、近邊那落迦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　次成最下八大地獄，還有諸大那落迦（八熱地獄），及獨一那落迦（孤獨地獄）、寒那落迦（八寒地獄）、近邊那落迦（八熱地獄門外的四種地獄）。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地五、一分鬼傍生處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科一分鬼傍生處，說明一分鬼與傍生處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復成一分鬼、傍生處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又形成一分鬼住的地方與畜生住的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、廣四洲3　天一、列名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣四洲，廣泛地說明四大洲，分三科；第一科列名，列出四大洲的名字。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四大洲者，謂南贍部洲、東毗提訶洲、西瞿陀尼洲、北拘盧洲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有四大洲，南邊是南贍部洲、東邊是毗提訶洲、西邊是瞿陀尼洲、北邊是拘盧洲。我們是住在南贍部洲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、辨相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨相，說明四大洲的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p145"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其贍部洲，形如車箱；毗提訶洲，形如半月；瞿陀尼洲，其形圓滿；北拘盧洲，其形四方。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　南贍部洲的形狀像車箱；東毗提訶洲，形狀像半個月亮；西瞿陀尼洲，形狀像圓形；北拘盧洲，形狀像四方形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、顯量</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯量，說明四大洲的量。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">贍部洲量，六千五百踰繕那；毗提訶洲量，七千踰繕那；瞿陀尼洲量，七千五百踰繕那；拘盧洲量，八千踰繕那。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　南贍部洲的量是六千五百踰繕那（由旬）；東毗提訶洲的量是七千踰繕那；西瞿陀尼洲量有七千五百踰繕那；北拘盧洲量有八千踰繕那。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、約有情辨9　戌一、八大龍王所住2　亥一、內海2　天一、標具德</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約有情辨，以眾生住處說明器世間，分九科；第一科八大龍王所住，說明八大龍王所住的地方，又分二科；第一科內海，說明內海，又分二科；第一科標具德，標內海具八支德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又七金山，其間有水，具八支德，名為內海。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又七金山環繞著蘇迷盧山，每座山之間有水，稱為內海，內海有八種功德，稱為八支德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又七金山其間有水具八支德名為內海者：俱舍論中分別世品作如是說：妙高為初，輪圍最後。中間八海，前七名內。七中皆具八功德水。一、甘，二、冷，三、軟，四、輕，五、清淨，六、不臭，七、飲時不損喉，八、飲已不傷腹。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《俱舍論‧分別世品》這樣說：妙高山就是蘇迷盧山，世間最初有蘇迷盧山，最後是輪圍山。輪圍山最後形成，四大洲與八中洲被輪圍山包圍。中間有八個海，前面七個稱為內海，七內海的水都具備有八功德。第一個是甘，水很甜。第二個是冷，第三個、軟，很柔軟，第四個很輕，第五個是清淨，第六個是不臭，第七個是飲時不損喉嚨，第八是喝完不傷腸胃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、舉龍眾3　地一、標列名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科舉龍眾，舉出住在內海的龍眾，分三科；第一科標列名，標列龍王的名字。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復成諸龍宮。有八大龍，并經劫住。謂持地龍王、歡喜近喜龍王、馬騾龍王、目支鄰陀龍王、意猛龍王、持國龍王、大黑龍王、黳羅葉龍王。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又形成諸龍宮。有八大龍王，可住經一劫。龍王住在龍宮，有八種龍王：持地龍王、歡喜近喜龍王、馬騾龍王、目支鄰陀龍王、意猛龍王、持國龍王、大黑龍王、黳羅葉龍王。龍王主下雨，能夠呼風喚雨。《大雲經祈雨壇法》說：如果一個地方乾旱很久，至誠請一切佛菩薩加持，晝夜虔誠讀此《大雲經》，或二人三人乃至七人更替讀誦，經聲不應間斷。亢旱之時，如是依法讀此《大雲經》，或經一日二日乃至七日，定降注甘雨。若災重不雨，更作必降甘雨。假使大海或有過限越潮，依此經作法轉讀，無不應效，應發願讀經所生功德迴向諸龍，願皆離諸苦難，發無上菩提心，為一切有情降注甘雨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p146"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、出作業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出作業，說明龍王所作的業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是諸龍王，由帝釋力，數與非天共相戰諍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些龍王，由帝釋天（地居天的最高天）統治，下令龍王和阿修羅（非天）共相戰諍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、辨種類2　玄一、正辨自類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨種類，說明龍王的種類，分二科；第一科正辨自類，正式說明龍眾的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其諸龍眾類有四種。謂卵生、胎生、濕生、化生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　龍王的種類有卵生的，在東南海的地方，胎生是住在南邊的內海，濕生住在西邊的內海，化生是住在北邊的內海。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、兼說鳥類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科兼說鳥類，兼說鳥類也有四生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">妙翅鳥中，四類亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因金翅鳥專吃龍王的龍子、龍女，也是有卵胎濕化生四類，也和龍王一樣分佈在東南西北四邊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、外海</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科外海，說明外海。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有餘水，在內海外，故名外海。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七金山有七個內海，外面還有一層海稱為外海。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、堅手神等所住2　亥一、出四級</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科堅手神等所住，說明堅手神等所住，分二科；第一科出四級，說明從蘇迷盧山開始向外有四個層級。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依蘇迷盧根，有四重級。從蘇迷盧初級，傍出一萬六千踰繕那量。即從此量半半漸減，如其次第，餘級應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依蘇迷盧根，有四重級。從蘇迷盧根即中間的海平面，向傍出一萬六千踰繕那（由旬）量，這是第一級。從此每一級漸漸減半，往外第二級就是往外八千踰繕那，再往外第三級是往外四千踰繕那，第四級是往外二千踰繕那，如此依次類推有四級。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、明彼住</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明彼住，說明堅手神等住在蘇迷盧山外四個層級。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有堅手神住最初級，血手神住第二級，常醉神住第三級，持鬘神住第四級。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從內向外，有堅手神住最初級，血手神住第二級，常醉神住第三級，持鬘神住第四級。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p147"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、藥叉所住</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科藥叉所住，說明藥叉的住處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">蘇迷盧頂四隅之上有四大峰，各高五百踰繕那量。有諸藥叉，謂金剛手止住其中。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘇迷盧山的頂端，四隅即東南角、西南角、東北角、西北角，向上有四大山峰，各高五百踰繕那量。有諸藥叉，指金剛手菩薩，是普賢菩薩的代表化身，止住其中。藥叉是住在蘇迷盧山的頂端。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、四天王等所住2　亥一、四天王</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科四天王等所住，說明四天王等所住，分二科；第一科四天王，說明四天王所住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又持雙山，於其四面有四王都。東南西北隨其次第，謂持國、增長、醜目、多聞四大天王之所居止。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在蘇迷盧山的旁邊有持雙山，四面有四天王的宮殿。東邊是持國天王、南邊是增長天王、西邊是醜目天王、北邊是多聞天王，四大天王是住在持雙山的四面上。持雙山是在蘇迷盧山的外圍，比蘇迷盧山矮一半。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、彼部落</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科彼部落，說明四大天王部落的住處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸餘金山，是彼四王村邑部落。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七金山，第一個稱為持雙山，是四天王所居。其他的金山，如毗那矺迦山乃至尼民達羅山，就是屬於四天王的村邑、部落。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌五、善住龍王所住3　亥一、出住處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科善住龍王所住，說明善住龍王所住的地方，分三科；第一科出住處，說明其住處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又近雪山，有大金崖，名非天脅，其量縱廣五十踰繕那，善住龍王常所居鎮，又天帝釋時來遊幸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　雪山是在南贍部洲的北邊。又靠近雪山有大金崖，名非天脅（非天即阿修羅），大金崖形狀像阿修羅的手臂一樣。其量縱廣（高與寬）五十踰繕那，善住龍王常居住在此，住在蘇迷盧山頂的帝釋天，也常來附近遊玩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋得名，解釋得名善住的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中有樹，名曰善住，多羅樹行，七重圍繞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　善住龍王住的地方有一棵樹，名為善住，旁邊有多羅樹一行行排列，七重圍繞著善住樹。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p148"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、顯受用2　天一、漫陀吉尼池</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯受用，說明善住龍王的受用，分二科；第一科漫陀吉尼池，介紹漫陀吉尼池。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有大池，名漫陀吉尼，五百小池以為眷屬。善住大龍與五百牝象前後圍繞，遊戲其池，隨欲變現，便入此池，採蓮華根以供所食。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大雪山附近還有一大池，稱為漫陀吉尼池，有五百小池塘如同其眷屬池。善住大龍王由五百母象一起前後圍繞，在池中遊戲，隨其所想變現，想要進就進入池中，以採蓮華的根作為食物。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、無熱大池2　地一、顯具德</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無熱大池，說明無熱大池，分二科；第一科顯具德，顯所具的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即於此側，有無熱大池，其量深廣各五十踰繕那；微細金沙遍布其底，八支德水彌滿其中，形色殊妙，端嚴喜見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　漫陀吉尼池的旁邊有一池，稱為無熱大池，其量深與寬各五十踰繕那；有很多微細金沙遍布池底，八支德水（甘、冷、軟、輕、清淨、不臭、飲時不損喉、飲已不傷腹）彌滿其中，形色殊妙，端正莊嚴，大家看了都很喜歡，沒有熱惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、出派流</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出派流，從無熱大池派流為四大河。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從此派流為四大河。一名殑伽，二名信度，三名私多，四名縛芻。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從此無熱大池分出四大河流。一名殑伽（恒河），二名信度（印度河），三名私多（奧克薩斯河），四名縛芻（查可薩提河）。在《金剛經》常說到殑伽大河，與現在的印度配合起來即指恒河。如對照現在的地理來看，蘇迷盧山即喜瑪拉雅山，靠近尼泊爾的位置，那個地方有龍王、帝釋天住在那裡，因為和印度很近，帝釋天常常下來聽佛陀說法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌六、帝釋等所住2　亥一、出住處2　天一、帝釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科帝釋等所住，說明帝釋等所住之處，分二科；第一科出住處，說出住處，又分二科；第一科帝釋，說明帝釋住蘇迷盧頂處中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，於蘇迷盧頂處中，建立帝釋天宮，縱廣十千踰繕那量。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　接下來，於蘇迷盧山的頂端，有帝釋天宮，縱廣一萬踰繕那。踰繕那到底是多少？玄奘法師的《西域記》卷2有說到：舊傳一踰繕那是四十里，但是印度人的習俗一踰繕那有三十里，而經典上說一踰繕那有十六里，每個地方說法不一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、諸天</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科諸天，說明帝釋天宮以外，還有其他諸天住在那裡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘之處，是彼諸天村邑聚落。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　帝釋天旁邊住的，就是諸天的村邑聚落。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、明住向2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明住向，說明住的方向，分二科；第一科標，標出四寶所成。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p149"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其山四面，對四大洲，四寶所成。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘇迷盧山四面，對著四大洲，由四種寶物所形成。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂對贍部洲，琉璃為面；對毗提訶，白銀為面；對瞿陀尼，黃金為面；對拘盧洲，頗胝為面。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對南贍部洲，是青琉璃為面；對東邊的毗提訶，是白銀為面；面對西瞿陀尼，是黃金為面；對北拘盧洲，頗胝（紅色）為面。這是說到帝釋跟諸天等所居住的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌七、輪王所行3　亥一、出彼路</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科輪王所行，說明輪王所居住的地方，分三科；第一科出彼路，說明輪王的路。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又贍部洲，循其邊際，有輪王路，真金所成，如四大王天有情膝量，沒住大海。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又循著南贍部洲的邊際，海底的深處有輪王的路，金輪王的路是金子所構成，像四大王天膝蓋那樣的高度，平日是沈在大海裡，是很深的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、明出現</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明出現，說明輪王路出現的時間。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若輪王出世，如彼膝量海水減焉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若轉輪聖王出世時，像四大王天膝蓋那樣高度的海水，全部會退落，南瞻部洲就浮現出真金作成的轉輪聖王的路。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、釋洲名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋洲名，解釋贍部洲的名稱由來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又無熱池南有一大樹，名為贍部，是故此洲從彼得名。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又無熱池南邊有一棵大樹，名字稱為贍部，所以此洲依贍部樹得名，稱為贍部洲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌八、妙翅諸鳥所住</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科妙翅諸鳥所住，說明妙翅諸鳥所住的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次於此北，有設拉末梨大樹叢林，四生種類妙翅諸鳥栖集其中。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在贍部洲的北邊，有設拉末梨大樹叢林，有胎卵濕化四生種類的妙翅諸鳥停留棲息其中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p150"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌九、羅剎所住</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科羅剎所住，說明羅剎所住的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此四大洲各二中洲以為眷屬。復有一洲，羅剎所住。</span></strong></span></span></p>
