<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此四大洲旁邊各有二個中洲以為它的眷屬。又有一洲，是羅剎所居住的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《俱舍論頌疏論本》卷11〈分別根品二之一〉說：「復有八中洲，是大洲眷屬。謂四大洲側，各有二中洲。贍部洲邊二中洲者：一遮末羅洲，此云貓牛；二筏羅遮末羅洲，此云勝貓牛。東勝身洲，邊二中洲者：一提訶洲，此云身；二毘提訶洲，此云勝身。西牛貨洲，邊二中洲者：一舍揥洲，此云諂；二嗢怛羅漫恒里拏洲，此云上儀。北俱盧洲，邊二中洲者：一矩拉婆洲，此云勝邊；二憍拉婆洲，此云有勝邊。此八中洲，皆人所住，人形短小，如此方侏儒。有說唯一洲，羅剎婆居，即是此方，遮末羅洲也。」根據《俱舍論頌疏論本》說南贍部洲邊之遮末羅洲為羅剎所住。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是介紹九種有情來世間居住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、一分有情世間2　酉一、人趣攝2　戌一、出現漸次2　亥一、劫初有情3　天一、略明生相2　地一、依處攝2　玄一、標感業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科一分有情世間，說明一分有情世間的相狀，分二科；第一科人趣攝，以人趣所攝，又分二科；第一科出現漸次，說明人趣出現的漸次，又分二科；第一科劫初有情，說明劫初有情，又分三科；第一科略明生相，要略說明劫初有情生出來的相貌，又分二科；第一科依處攝，依處所攝，又分二科；第一科標感業，標出感得的業力。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是器世間成已，有諸有情從極淨光天眾同分沒，來生此中。餘如前說。此皆由彼感劫初業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是器世間成就以後，就會有有情從極淨光天（二禪天最高天）壽盡、業盡、福盡死了，投生來到世間。這些有情由於有劫初業的福報，感得此時來人間受生。最先開始是無量壽，身有光明又能飛等，其餘如前文所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、釋增上</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋增上，解釋劫初業最勝微妙，唯於此時此業感果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此業第一，最勝微妙，欲界所攝；唯於此時此業感果，非於餘時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　劫初業是欲界眾生最好的業力，在劫初時有情苦少一點，樂多一點，所以是最勝微妙。而且只有在這個時候才會下生人間，其他的時候沒有這個業果，它有一些特別的特性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、自體攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科自體攝，說明劫初有情自體所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">爾時有情名劫初者。又彼有色從意所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那時的有情名劫初者。又劫初有情的有色身是從心意所化生，從第六意識所產生的。他們有光明、道德、智慧，不是母腹所生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、廣指經說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣指經說，廣指如經所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切，如經廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是劫初有情的一切相狀，如經上廣說。經典上有說劫初有情的情況，《增壹阿含經．七日品》中也有介紹。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、顯無攝受</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯無攝受，顯示劫初有情沒有攝受家宅及諸聚落。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p151"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於爾時，未有家宅及諸聚落。一切大地面皆平正。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　劫初有情最剛開始，沒有房子也沒有聚落。一切大地表面都很平正。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、此後有情2　天一、無攝受位</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科此後有情，說明此後有情，分二科；第一科無攝受位，說明於地味無攝受位。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自此以後，由諸有情福業力故，有地味生。如是漸次，地餅、林藤，不種粳稻，自然出現，無糠無籺；次有粳稻，有籺有糠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　自此以後，由於有情福報業力的增上緣，有地味生，白天採，晚上又長出來，不用儲藏。《增壹阿含經》有說，這地味像甜葡萄酒的味道。如是漸漸地，地上長出餅、林藤可以吃。那時不用種粳稻（粳是不黏而晚熟的稻），自然出現，米沒有殼也沒有粗或細的米屑；接下來長出的稻米，有殼也有細米屑。這是無攝受位當時的情況。就是大家想到就吃，沒有想到將它儲存起來。據說當時，地味日間採，夜間又長出來，夜間採，日間又長出來，所以不用去採起來存在家裡，因為隨時採隨時都有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、有攝受位2　地一、攝受粳稻2　玄一、標攝受</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有攝受位，說明於地味有攝受位，分二科；第一科攝受粳稻，又分二科；第一科標攝受，標出攝受相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復處處粳稻叢生，於是有情方現攝受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　接下來到處都有稻米產生，於是有一些有情將這些食物收藏起來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、廣受用2　黃一、受用飲食2　宇一、明過患3　宙一、光明滅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣受用，廣說受用的相狀，分二科；第一科受用飲食，說明受用飲食，又分二科；第一科明過患，說明受用飲食有三種過患，又分三科；第一科光明滅，令光明滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次由受用味等資緣，有情之類惡色便起，光明遂滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因受用地味，使有情的身色變成不好，光明就沒有了。這是第一種過患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙二、身沈重</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科身沈重，令身沈重。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其多食者，惡色逾增，身極沈重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　吃比較多的人，身色更不好，而且身體很沉重。這是第二種過患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙三、地味沒</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科地味沒，令地味消失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此諸有情互相輕毀，惡法現行。由此因緣，所有味等漸沒於地。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情互相毀謗要奪取食物，惡法就因此現行，有的甚至還去偷盜。由此因緣，所有地味等漸漸無法從地上長出來。這是第三種過患。《增壹阿含經．七日品》說到，他們是如何的造作惡法，當時有人懶惰，不想天天去採，二天採一次，就告訴其他的有情，另一個有情就存四天的食物，又另一個有情就採了八天的食物存在家裡；於是惡行漸起，大家互相比較，愈採愈多；不夠了，就去偷他人的。第一個偷的人被抓到，第二個人去偷時，被抓到時趕不走，就打起架來。因為打架的關係，就選一個人管理田地。這管理人剎帝利就出現，來管理田。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最初從光音天來時，本來大家都是男性。但吃了地味後，有一種人貪欲比較強就變女性。想作欲的事情，又造房子來隱蔽自己。這剎帝利管理很嚴格，有一次抓到小偷時，很氣，就將他殺掉，於是開始有殺生惡行。先有淫欲，再有偷盜，又有殺生的事。有一部分光音天來的人覺得有淫欲、偷盜、與殺生的事不好，感覺需要修行，這一部分人就放棄妻子、兒女，出來修行，這些人稱為婆羅門，於是婆羅門種姓就出現了。剎帝利就宣佈，從今以後大家都不可偷盜。有一類人說要活下來，就要來做貿易的事情，於是有吠舍種姓的有情出現，負責買賣。也有人要自食其力做事情，於是首陀羅（耕田植種） 種姓有情就出現了。這四種種姓，據佛陀說，剎帝利、婆羅門、吠舍、和首陀羅四種姓從以前就有，可是他們是從同一光音天來的。不是像外道說，從口生出就是婆羅門，是最高級的種姓，從肚子生出來是吠舍等等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、指經說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科指經說，指如經上廣說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p152"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如經廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如經上廣說。《增壹阿含經》有廣泛地說明劫初有情的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、受用婬欲3　宇一、起愛染</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科受用婬欲，說明受用婬欲，分三科；第一科起愛染，說明有情生起愛染。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復從此緣，諸有情類更相顧眄，便起愛染。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於他們有吃東西，食色為性，就有有情互相顧視，生起愛戀染著之心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、起二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科起二根，說明感男女業故起二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="45125:1397"></a>次由能感男女業故，一分有情男根生起，一分有情女根生起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於心裡有愛染心，有感得男女的業力，一部分有情有男根生起，一部分有情有女根生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇三、自隱蔽</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科自隱蔽，又造室宅隱蔽自己的邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">遞相陵犯，起諸邪行，遂為他人之所訶訾，方造室宅以自隱蔽。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有男女互相邪行，為其他人訶責不該做這種事，於是他們就造了房室以自隱蔽邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、攝受其地2　玄一、舉攝受因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科攝受其地，攝受土地，分二科；第一科舉攝受因，舉攝受的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復由攝受粳稻因故，遂於其地復起攝受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為要將粳稻藏起來當做食物，接下來占據土地，才能攝受這些稻米。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、顯彼增上3　黃一、生不與取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯彼增上，顯攝受增上的作用，分三科；第一科生不與取，生出偷盜的行為。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此緣已，更相爭奪，不與取法從此而生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有這些攝受土地的因緣，由此因緣，更相爭奪，不與取法（偷盜）就此而生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、立司契者</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科立司契者，安立司契者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即由此緣，立司契者，彼最初王名大等意。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為偷盜使大家不勝其擾，由於這個因緣，就派一個人為管理者，這管理人最初的名字是大等意。大等，即大眾起等，意樂共同，立以為尊。就是大眾生起共同相等的意樂，安立這個人最為尊貴，出來管理大家的事務。在《增一阿含經．七日品》中說這個人就是剎帝利。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="02p153"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃三、四姓出現2　宇一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科四姓出現，說明四姓</span></span></span></div>
